fa-angle-right"></i></i><span>What is AppData folder in Windows and how to clean it up?</span> </div> <div class="container container-single container-single-magazine penci_sidebar right-sidebar penci-enable-lightbox"> <div id="main"> <div class="theiaStickySidebar"> <article id="post-20007" class="post type-post status-publish"> <div class="header-standard header-classic single-header"> <div class="penci-standard-cat"><span class="cat"><a class="penci-cat-name penci-cat-332" href="https://theitbros.com/windows/" rel="category tag follow noopener noreferrer" data-wpel-link="internal" target="_self"><span>Windows</span></a></span></div> <h1 class="post-title single-post-title entry-title">What is AppData folder in Windows and how to clean it up?</h1> <div class="penci-hide-tagupdated"> <span class="author-italic author vcard">by <a class="author-url url fn n" href="https://theitbros.com/author/administrator/" data-wpel-link="internal" target="_self" rel="follow noopener noreferrer">Cyril Kardashevsky</a> </span> <time class="entry-date published" datetime="2025-09-08T11:24:00-04:00">September 8, 2025</time> </div> <div class="post-box-meta-single"> <span class="author-post byline"><span class="author vcard">written by <a class="author-url url fn n" href="https://theitbros.com/author/administrator/" data-wpel-link="internal" target="_self" rel="follow noopener noreferrer">Cyril Kardashevsky</a> </span> </span> <span><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2025-09-08T11:24:00-04:00">September 8, 2025</time></span> <span><i class="penci-post-countview-number">11.7K</i> views</span> </div> </div> <div class="post-entry blockquote-style-1 "> <div class="inner-post-entry entry-content" id="penci-post-entry-inner"> <i class="penci-post-countview-number-check" style="display:none">11.7K</i> <main id="main-content-area"> <p>The <strong>AppData</strong> <strong>(App</strong>lication <strong>Data) </strong>folder in Windows is used by apps to store their data, settings, configuration files, and caches. Over time, it can become bloated with unnecessary files, which can lead to slower performance and take up free space on your hard drive.</p> <div style="height:10px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div> <div id="ez-toc-container" class="ez-toc-v2_0_81 counter-hierarchy ez-toc-counter ez-toc-white ez-toc-container-direction"> <div class="ez-toc-title-container"> <p class="ez-toc-title" style="cursor:inherit">Contents</p> <span class="ez-toc-title-toggle"><a href="#" class="ez-toc-pull-right ez-toc-btn ez-toc-btn-xs ez-toc-btn-default ez-toc-toggle" aria-label="Toggle Table of Content"><span class="ez-toc-js-icon-con"><span><span class="eztoc-hide" style="display:none;">Toggle</span><span class="ez-toc-icon-toggle-span"><svg style="fill: #999;color:#999" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="list-377408" width="20px" height="20px" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M6 6H4v2h2V6zm14 0H8v2h12V6zM4 11h2v2H4v-2zm16 0H8v2h12v-2zM4 16h2v2H4v-2zm16 0H8v2h12v-2z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg><svg style="fill: #999;color:#999" class="arrow-unsorted-368013" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="10px" height="10px" viewBox="0 0 24 24" version="1.2" baseProfile="tiny"><path d="M18.2 9.3l-6.2-6.3-6.2 6.3c-.2.2-.3.4-.3.7s.1.5.3.7c.2.2.4.3.7.3h11c.3 0 .5-.1.7-.3.2-.2.3-.5.3-.7s-.1-.5-.3-.7zM5.8 14.7l6.2 6.3 6.2-6.3c.2-.2.3-.5.3-.7s-.1-.5-.3-.7c-.2-.2-.4-.3-.7-.3h-11c-.3 0-.5.1-.7.3-.2.2-.3.5-.3.7s.1.5.3.7z"/></svg></span></span></span></a></span></div> <nav><ul class='ez-toc-list ez-toc-list-level-1 eztoc-toggle-hide-by-default'><li class='ez-toc-page-1 ez-toc-heading-level-2'><a class="ez-toc-link ez-toc-heading-1" href="#What_is_the_AppData_Folder_in_Windows">What is the AppData Folder in Windows</a><ul class='ez-toc-list-level-3'><li class='ez-toc-heading-level-3'><a class="ez-toc-link ez-toc-heading-2" href="#Default_AppData_Folder_Location">Default AppData Folder Location</a></li><li class='ez-toc-page-1 ez-toc-heading-level-3'><a class="ez-toc-link ez-toc-heading-3" href="#Local_LocalLow_and_Roaming_Explained">Local, LocalLow, and Roaming Explained</a></li></ul></li><li class='ez-toc-page-1 ez-toc-heading-level-2'><a class="ez-toc-link ez-toc-heading-4" href="#How_to_Safely_Clean_the_AppData_Folder">How to Safely Clean the AppData Folder</a><ul class='ez-toc-list-level-3'><li class='ez-toc-heading-level-3'><a class="ez-toc-link ez-toc-heading-5" href="#Check_AppData_Size_with_PowerShell">Check AppData Size with PowerShell</a></li><li class='ez-toc-page-1 ez-toc-heading-level-3'><a class="ez-toc-link ez-toc-heading-6" href="#Analyze_AppData_Space_with_WinDirStat">Analyze AppData Space with WinDirStat</a></li><li class='ez-toc-page-1 ez-toc-heading-level-3'><a class="ez-toc-link ez-toc-heading-7" href="#Identify_Large_UWP_AppData_Packages">Identify Large UWP AppData Packages</a></li></ul></li><li class='ez-toc-page-1 ez-toc-heading-level-2'><a class="ez-toc-link ez-toc-heading-8" href="#Methods_to_Clean_Up_AppData_Folder">Methods to Clean Up AppData Folder</a><ul class='ez-toc-list-level-3'><li class='ez-toc-heading-level-3'><a class="ez-toc-link ez-toc-heading-9" href="#Clear_AppData_via_Windows_Settings">Clear AppData via Windows Settings</a></li><li class='ez-toc-page-1 ez-toc-heading-level-3'><a class="ez-toc-link ez-toc-heading-10" href="#Manually_Delete_Temp_Files_in_AppData">Manually Delete Temp Files in AppData</a></li><li class='ez-toc-page-1 ez-toc-heading-level-3'><a class="ez-toc-link ez-toc-heading-11" href="#Clean_AppData_Using_PowerShell">Clean AppData Using PowerShell</a></li></ul></li><li class='ez-toc-page-1 ez-toc-heading-level-2'><a class="ez-toc-link ez-toc-heading-12" href="#Advanced_AppData_Management">Advanced AppData Management</a><ul class='ez-toc-list-level-3'><li class='ez-toc-heading-level-3'><a class="ez-toc-link ez-toc-heading-13" href="#Move_the_Roaming_Folder_Mapping_to_Another_Drive">Move the Roaming Folder Mapping to Another Drive</a></li></ul></li></ul></nav></div> <h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="What_is_the_AppData_Folder_in_Windows"></span>What is the AppData Folder in Windows<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2> <p>Each Windows user profile contains a hidden folder called AppData. It contains user settings, caches, temporary files, and other data required by apps for proper operation and personalization.</p> <div style="height:10px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div> <h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Default_AppData_Folder_Location"></span>Default AppData Folder Location<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3> <p>The default location of the AppData folder in Windows is &lt;OS_Drive&gt;:\Users\&lt;Username&gt;\AppData.</p> <p>You can quickly navigate to this directory using the following command in the Run dialog or File Explorer address bar:</p> <pre class="wp-block-preformatted">%userprofile%\AppData</pre> <div class="wp-block-image"> <figure class="aligncenter"><img fetchpriority="high" decoding="async" width="420" height="236" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20420%20236'%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/clear-appdata.png" alt="Command %userprofile%\AppData in Run dialog box" class=" penci-lazy wp-image-40451" title="Command %userprofile%\AppData in Run dialog box"/></figure> </div> <div style="height:10px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div> <h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Local_LocalLow_and_Roaming_Explained"></span>Local, LocalLow, and Roaming Explained<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3> <p>There are three subfolders within the AppData folder: <em>Local</em>, <em>LocalLow</em>, and <em>Roaming</em>.</p> <ul class="wp-block-list"> <li><strong>Local</strong> – contains device-specific settings, temporary files, local caches. This folder is usually quite large, so app developers don&#8217;t intend to sync its contents with other computers during user profile synchronization. You can access this directory using the <a href="https://theitbros.com/environment-variables-powershell/" target="_self" data-wpel-link="internal" rel="follow noopener noreferrer">environment variable</a> <strong>%LOCALAPPDATA%</strong>);</li> <li><strong>LocalLow </strong>– used for low-integrity application data, which is only available in an isolated environment. For example, when a browser is running in Incognito mode, it uses the LocalLow folder to prevent access to user data stored in other folders.</li> <li><strong>Roaming</strong> – it stores <a data-wpil-monitor-id="30" href="https://theitbros.com/user-profile-service-failed-the-sign-in/" data-wpel-link="internal" target="_self" rel="follow noopener noreferrer">user profile</a> application settings and data that can be transferred from one computer to another (environment variable <strong>%APPDATA%</strong>). This folder can be used in <a href="https://theitbros.com/configuring-windows-roaming-user-profiles-in-active-directory/" target="_self" data-wpel-link="internal" rel="follow noopener noreferrer">roaming profiles </a>or user profile disks in an RDS environment.</li> </ul> <div class="wp-block-image"> <figure class="aligncenter"><img decoding="async" width="556" height="195" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20556%20195'%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/clean-appdata-folder.png" alt="Screenshot of Windows AppData folder location in File Explorer" class=" penci-lazy wp-image-40452" title="Screenshot of Windows AppData folder location in File Explorer" data-srcset="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/clean-appdata-folder.png 556w, https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/clean-appdata-folder-545x191.png 545w" sizes="(max-width: 556px) 100vw, 556px"/></figure> </div> <div style="height:10px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div> <h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="How_to_Safely_Clean_the_AppData_Folder"></span>How to Safely Clean the AppData Folder<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2> <p>Apps installed on a computer use the AppData folder to store their data. This folder can grow uncontrollably over time and consume all available storage space.</p> <p>If your computer is running low on <a href="https://theitbros.com/how-to-get-free-disk-space-using-powershell/" data-wpil-monitor-id="31" data-wpel-link="internal" target="_self" rel="follow noopener noreferrer">disk space</a>, one of the places to check for potential cleanup is the <strong>AppData</strong> directory.</p> <p>Even more importantly, uninstalling an app typically doesn&#8217;t remove its data files from the AppData folder. As a result, the AppData folder fills up with unnecessary files and folders.</p> <div style="height:10px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div> <h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Check_AppData_Size_with_PowerShell"></span>Check AppData Size with PowerShell<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3> <p>To get the size of the Local, LocalLow and Roaming folders in AppData, you can use the following PowerShell script:</p> <pre class="wp-block-preformatted">$AppDataPath = "$env:USERPROFILE\AppData"

$folders = @("Local", "LocalLow", "Roaming")

foreach ($folder in $folders) {

$path = Join-Path -Path $AppDataPath -ChildPath $folder

$sizeBytes = (Get-ChildItem -Path $path -Recurse -Force -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue | Measure-Object -Property Length -Sum).Sum

$sizeMB = [math]::Round($sizeBytes / 1MB, 2)

Write-Output "${folder}: $sizeMB MB"

}</pre> <p>The script calculated the total size of the files in each folder recursively and displayed the results on the screen.</p> <div class="wp-block-image"> <figure class="aligncenter"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="326" height="134" src="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/word-image-20007-3.png" alt="how to clean appdata folder windows 11" class="wp-image-40454" title="how to clean appdata folder windows 11"/></figure> </div> <div style="height:10px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div> <h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Analyze_AppData_Space_with_WinDirStat"></span>Analyze AppData Space with WinDirStat<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3> <p>If you prefer graphical tools for analyzing disk space usage in Windows, try the <strong>WinDirStat</strong> tool<strong>. It can </strong>be installed using the built-in WinGet package manager:</p> <pre class="wp-block-preformatted">winget install --id=WinDirStat.WinDirStat -e</pre> <div class="wp-block-image"> <figure class="aligncenter"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="540" height="47" src="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/clean-appdata.png" alt="appdata folder too big" class="wp-image-40455" title="appdata folder too big"/></figure> </div> <p>In this example, you can see that the size of the AppData folder is about 21 GB. The graphical folder map in WinDirStat allows you to quickly find files and folders that are taking up a lot of free space. For example, I quickly found a large VHDX image left over from experimenting with WSL in the \AppData\Local\Packages folder.</p> <div class="wp-block-image"> <figure class="aligncenter"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="717" height="733" src="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/appdata-folder-too-big.png" alt="Example of large AppData Local Packages folder" class="wp-image-40456" title="Example of large AppData Local Packages folder" srcset="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/appdata-folder-too-big.png 717w, https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/appdata-folder-too-big-545x557.png 545w, https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/appdata-folder-too-big-585x598.png 585w" sizes="(max-width: 717px) 100vw, 717px"/></figure> </div> <p>The directory that usually takes up the most space in the AppData folder is <strong>AppData\Local\Packages</strong>. This folder contains user data for Universal Windows Platform (UWP) apps installed through the Microsoft Store or MSIX packages. It contains settings files, caches, and application and user data for specific apps.</p> <div style="height:10px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div> <h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Identify_Large_UWP_AppData_Packages"></span>Identify Large UWP AppData Packages<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3> <p>Run the following PowerShell script to display top 10 largest app folders in the AppData\Local\Packages directory:</p> <pre class="wp-block-preformatted">$packagesPath = "$env:USERPROFILE\AppData\Local\Packages"

$folderSizes = Get-ChildItem -Path $packagesPath -Directory | ForEach-Object {

$size = (Get-ChildItem $_.FullName -Recurse -Force -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue | Measure-Object -Property Length -Sum).Sum

[PSCustomObject]@{

Name = $_.Name

SizeMB = [math]::Round($size / 1MB, 2)

}

}

$folderSizes | Sort-Object SizeMB -Descending | Select-Object -First 10</pre> <div class="wp-block-image"> <figure class="aligncenter"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="571" height="177" src="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/word-image-20007-6.png" alt="PowerShell script showing top 10 largest UWP app folders" class="wp-image-40457" title="PowerShell script showing top 10 largest UWP app folders" srcset="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/word-image-20007-6.png 571w, https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/word-image-20007-6-545x169.png 545w" sizes="(max-width: 571px) 100vw, 571px"/></figure> </div> <p>The names of the folders in the Packages directory are unique identifiers for UWP apps that are either installed from the Microsoft Store or preinstalled in Windows.</p> <p>You can display information about the Microsoft Store app by its folder name.</p> <pre class="wp-block-preformatted">Get-AppxPackage | where PackageFamilyName -eq CanonicalGroupLimited.Ubuntu24.04LTS_79rhkp1fndgsc</pre> <div class="wp-block-image"> <figure class="aligncenter"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="589" height="289" src="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/word-image-20007-7.png" alt="appdata folder is huge" class="wp-image-40458" title="appdata folder is huge" srcset="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/word-image-20007-7.png 589w, https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/word-image-20007-7-545x267.png 545w, https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/word-image-20007-7-585x287.png 585w" sizes="(max-width: 589px) 100vw, 589px"/></figure> </div> <p><strong>Is it safe to manually delete the contents of the Packages folder?</strong> It is generally <strong>not recommended</strong> to manually delete the contents of this folder, as doing so may result in the loss of settings and data. Many Microsoft Store apps offer an option to clear the cache or data in their settings. This is the safest option.</p> <p>As an alternative, you can clear the UWP app data via <strong>Settings</strong> &gt; <strong>Apps</strong> &gt; <em>APP NAME</em> &gt; <strong>Advanced Options</strong> &gt; <strong>Reset</strong>.</p> <div class="wp-block-image"> <figure class="aligncenter"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="762" height="632" src="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/word-image-20007-8.png" alt="why is my appdata folder so large" class="wp-image-40459" title="why is my appdata folder so large" srcset="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/word-image-20007-8.png 762w, https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/word-image-20007-8-545x452.png 545w, https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/word-image-20007-8-585x485.png 585w" sizes="(max-width: 762px) 100vw, 762px"/></figure> </div> <div class="wp-block-image"> <figure class="aligncenter"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="525" height="254" src="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/word-image-20007-9.png" alt="appdata/local/packages" class="wp-image-40460" title="appdata/local/packages"/></figure> </div> <p>This will clean up the app&#8217;s data in the Packages folder.</p> <div style="height:10px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div> <h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Methods_to_Clean_Up_AppData_Folder"></span>Methods to Clean Up AppData Folder<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2> <h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Clear_AppData_via_Windows_Settings"></span>Clear AppData via Windows Settings<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3> <p>One way is to use the <strong>Settings</strong> app to remove temporary files, which include the safe-to-delete items in the AppData folder.</p> <ol class="wp-block-list"> <li>Press <strong>WIN+I</strong> to launch the <strong>Settings</strong> app.</li> <li>Click <strong>System → Storage</strong>.<br><figure><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" title="appdata taking up a lot of space" width="650" height="508" class="aligncenter wp-image-40461" src="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/appdata-folder-taking-up-space.png" alt="appdata taking up a lot of space" srcset="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/appdata-folder-taking-up-space.png 1021w, https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/appdata-folder-taking-up-space-545x426.png 545w, https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/appdata-folder-taking-up-space-950x743.png 950w, https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/appdata-folder-taking-up-space-768x600.png 768w, https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/appdata-folder-taking-up-space-585x457.png 585w" sizes="(max-width: 650px) 100vw, 650px"/></figure></li> <li>Click “<strong>Temporary files.</strong>”<br><figure><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" title="Storage settings interface with temporary file categories" width="512" height="310" class="aligncenter wp-image-40462 size-full" src="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/how-to-clean-appdata-folder-windows.png" alt="Storage settings interface with temporary file categories"></figure></li> <li>You’ll see a list of temporary file categories. Select the ones you want to clean up, including the Temporary Internet Files, and click the “<strong>Remove files</strong>” button.<br><figure><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" title="Windows Settings → Storage temporary files cleanup option" width="472" height="723" class="aligncenter wp-image-40463 size-full" src="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/how-to-clean-appdata.png" alt="Windows Settings → Storage temporary files cleanup option"></figure></li> </ol> <div style="height:10px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div> <h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Manually_Delete_Temp_Files_in_AppData"></span>Manually Delete Temp Files in AppData<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3> <p>Once you have closed all running applications, you can safely delete the temporary files in the AppData folder manually. Deleting the contents of the %LOCALAPPDATA%\Temp folder is always safe.</p> <ol class="wp-block-list"> <li>Open the File Explorer, paste <strong>%temp%</strong> in the address box;</li> <li>The Temp folder should open in the current user’s profile. (%Username%\AppData\Local\Temp). In our case, the size of the Temp folder is about 4GB;</li> <li>Delete all (or selected) files from Temp folder; <figure><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" title="File Explorer Temp folder contents in AppData Local" width="650" height="423" class="aligncenter wp-image-40464" src="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/appdata-cleanup.png" alt="File Explorer Temp folder contents in AppData Local" srcset="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/appdata-cleanup.png 799w, https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/appdata-cleanup-545x355.png 545w, https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/appdata-cleanup-768x500.png 768w, https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/appdata-cleanup-585x381.png 585w" sizes="(max-width: 650px) 100vw, 650px"/></figure></li> <li>Some files cannot be deleted because they are being used by other programs—which is normal. When you receive such a notification, check the “<strong>Do this for all current items</strong>” box and click <strong>Skip</strong>.<br><figure><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" title="appdata local packages" width="447" height="289" class="aligncenter wp-image-40465 size-full" src="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/windows-appdata-folder-too-large.png" alt="appdata local packages"></figure></li> </ol> <div style="height:10px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div> <h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Clean_AppData_Using_PowerShell"></span>Clean AppData Using PowerShell<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3> <p>You can also use the PowerShell one-liner to quickly clean up the temporary files in the AppData folder:</p> <pre class="wp-block-preformatted">Remove-Item `

-Path "$env:temp\*" `

-Recurse -Confirm:$false `

-ErrorAction SilentlyContinue `

-Verbose</pre> <div class="wp-block-image"> <figure class="aligncenter"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="974" height="428" src="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/clean-up-appdata.png" alt="PowerShell command to remove Temp files automatically" class="wp-image-40466" title="PowerShell command to remove Temp files automatically" srcset="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/clean-up-appdata.png 974w, https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/clean-up-appdata-545x239.png 545w, https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/clean-up-appdata-950x417.png 950w, https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/clean-up-appdata-768x337.png 768w, https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/clean-up-appdata-585x257.png 585w" sizes="(max-width: 974px) 100vw, 974px"/></figure> </div> <div style="height:10px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div> <h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Advanced_AppData_Management"></span>Advanced AppData Management<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2> <h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Move_the_Roaming_Folder_Mapping_to_Another_Drive"></span>Move the Roaming Folder Mapping to Another Drive<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3> <p>Rather than playing catch-up with the size of the AppData folder, it may be more practical to move the AppData folder to another drive with more space.</p> <ol class="wp-block-list"> <li>Navigate to the AppData folder and open the <strong>Roaming</strong> folder properties;</li> <li>Switch to the <strong>Location</strong> tab, enter the new <strong>Roaming</strong> folder location, and click <strong>OK</strong>. In this example, I’ll move the Roaming folder location to the X drive and retain the folder structure.<br><figure><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" title="Changing AppData Roaming folder path to another drive" width="360" height="495" class="aligncenter wp-image-40467 size-full" src="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/how-to-clear-appdata.png" alt="Changing AppData Roaming folder path to another drive"></figure></li> <li>Click <strong>Yes</strong> to automatically create the new location if it doesn’t exist.<br><figure><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" title="packages folder in appdata" width="397" height="176" class="aligncenter wp-image-40468 size-full" src="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/windows-clean-appdata.png" alt="packages folder in appdata"></figure></li> <li>Click <strong>Yes</strong> to move all files to the new location.<br><figure><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" title="Confirmation prompt when moving Roaming folder" width="555" height="205" class="aligncenter wp-image-40469 size-full" src="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/windows-clear-appdata.png" alt="Confirmation prompt when moving Roaming folder" srcset="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/windows-clear-appdata.png 555w, https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/windows-clear-appdata-545x201.png 545w" sizes="(max-width: 555px) 100vw, 555px"/></figure></li> <li>Wait for the file copy to finish.<br><figure><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" title="File copy progress when moving AppData folder" width="448" height="162" class="aligncenter wp-image-40470 size-full" src="https://theitbros.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/appdata-local-folder-huge.png" alt="File copy progress when moving AppData folder"></figure></li> <li>Restart computer and check if your apps are working properly. You can then rename the old <strong>Roaming</strong> folder to something like <strong>Roaming.bak</strong> and delete the original folder after a few days.</li> </ol> </main><div class='code-block     (function() {
        document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
            // Исправляем поле Email (селектор input.wpsf-email)
            var emailInput = document.querySelector('input.wpsf-email');
            if (emailInput && !emailInput.getAttribute('aria-label')) {
                emailInput.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Enter your email address');
            }
            
            // На всякий случай проверяем другие анонимные поля ввода
            var allInputs = document.querySelectorAll('input[type="email"], input[type="text"]');
            allInputs.forEach(function(input) {
                if (!input.getAttribute('id') && !input.getAttribute('aria-label') && input.getAttribute('placeholder')) {
                    input.setAttribute('aria-label', input.getAttribute('placeholder'));
                }
            });

var menuhbh_mobile = document.querySelector(".button-menu-mobile");

    menuhbh_mobile.addEventListener('click', function () {
        if (window.jQuery) {
            return false;
        }
        if (menuhbh_mobile.classList.contains('header-builder')) {
            document.body.classList.toggle("open-mobile-builder-sidebar-nav");
        } else {
            document.body.classList.toggle("open-sidebar-nav");
        }
    });
}

var menuhbh_search = document.querySelector(".pcheader-icon a.search-click");
if (menuhbh_search !== null) {
    menuhbh_search.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
        if (window.jQuery) {
            return false;
        }
        var closet = this.closest('.wrapper-boxed'),
            pbcloset = this.closest('.penci_nav_col'),
            sform = document.querySelector('.show-search');

        if (closet.classList.contains('header-search-style-showup')) {
            this.classList.toggle('active');
            sform.classList.toggle('active');
        } else {
            this.classList.toggle('fade');
            sform.classList.toggle('fade');
        }

        var opentimeout = setTimeout(function () {
            closet.querySelector('.search-input').focus();
            if (pbcloset !== null && !!pbcloset.querySelector('.search-input')) {
                pbcloset.querySelector('.search-input').focus();
            }
        }, 200, function () {
            clearTimeout(opentimeout);
        });

        e.stopPropagation();
        return false;
    });
}

function penci_check_isValidHttpUrl(string) {
    let url;

    try {
        url = new URL(string);
    } catch (_) {
        return false;
    }

    return url.protocol === "http:" || url.protocol === "https:";
}


var links = document.querySelectorAll("a");
if (links !== null) {
    links.forEach((link) => {
        link.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
            if (window.jQuery) {
                return false;
            }
            var linkurl = this.getAttribute('href');
            if (linkurl !== null && penci_check_isValidHttpUrl(linkurl)) {
                window.location.href = linkurl;
            }
        });
        link.addEventListener('ontouchstart', function (e) {
            if (window.jQuery) {
                return false;
            }
            var linkurl = this.getAttribute('href');
            if (linkurl !== null && penci_check_isValidHttpUrl(linkurl)) {
                window.location.href = linkurl;
            }
        });
    });
}
